     1	"""
     2	Result classes for nirs4all API.
     3	
     4	These dataclasses wrap the outputs from pipeline execution, prediction,
     5	and explanation operations, providing convenient accessor methods.
     6	
     7	Classes:
     8	    RunResult: Result from nirs4all.run()
     9	    PredictResult: Result from nirs4all.predict()
    10	    ExplainResult: Result from nirs4all.explain()
    11	
    12	Phase 1 Implementation (v0.6.0):
    13	    - RunResult: Full implementation with best, best_score, top(), export()
    14	    - PredictResult: Full implementation with values, to_dataframe()
    15	    - ExplainResult: Full implementation with values, feature attributions
    16	"""
    17	
    18	from __future__ import annotations
    19	
    20	import contextlib
    21	import threading
    22	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    23	from pathlib import Path
    24	from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any, cast
    25	
    26	import numpy as np
    27	
    28	from nirs4all.core.logging import get_logger
    29	
    30	if TYPE_CHECKING:
    31	    from nirs4all.data.predictions import Predictions
    32	    from nirs4all.pipeline import PipelineRunner
    33	    from nirs4all.pipeline.execution.refit.config_extractor import RefitConfig
    34	    from nirs4all.pipeline.execution.refit.model_selector import PerModelSelection
    35	
    36	logger = get_logger(__name__)
    37	
    38	@dataclass
    39	class ModelRefitResult:
    40	    """Per-model refit result metadata.
    41	
    42	    Captures the refit outcome for a single model node in the pipeline.
    43	    For Phase 2 (non-stacking), there is only one model node, so
    44	    ``RunResult.models`` will contain exactly one entry.
    45	
    46	    Attributes:
    47	        model_name: Name of the model (e.g. ``"PLSRegression"``).
    48	        final_entry: The refit prediction entry (``fold_id="final"``).
    49	        cv_entry: The best CV prediction entry for this model.
    50	        final_score: Test score from the refit model.
    51	        cv_score: Best validation score from CV.
    52	        metric: Metric name used for evaluation.
    53	    """
    54	
    55	    model_name: str = ""
    56	    final_entry: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    57	    cv_entry: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    58	    final_score: float | None = None
    59	    cv_score: float | None = None
    60	    metric: str = ""
    61	
    62	class LazyModelRefitResult:
    63	    """Lazy per-model refit result that triggers refit on first access.
    64	
    65	    Wraps a :class:`PerModelSelection` and defers the actual refit
    66	    execution until a property requiring the result (e.g. ``.score``,
    67	    ``.final_entry``, ``.export()``) is accessed.
    68	
    69	    After the first access, the result is cached so subsequent accesses
    70	    return instantly.
    71	
    72	    If the underlying resources (artifact registry, step cache) have
    73	    been destroyed by the time of access, the lazy refit re-executes
    74	    from scratch.
    75	
    76	    Attributes:
    77	        model_name: Name of the model.
    78	        selection: The PerModelSelection metadata from the CV phase.
    79	    """
    80	
    81	    def __init__(
    82	        self,
    83	        model_name: str,
    84	        selection: PerModelSelection,
    85	        refit_config: RefitConfig,
    86	        dataset: Any,
    87	        context: Any,
    88	        runtime_context: Any,
    89	        artifact_registry: Any,
    90	        executor: Any,
    91	        prediction_store: Any,
    92	    ) -> None:
    93	        self.model_name = model_name
    94	        self.selection = selection
    95	        self._refit_config = refit_config
    96	        self._dataset = dataset
    97	        self._context = context
    98	        self._runtime_context = runtime_context
    99	        self._artifact_registry = artifact_registry
   100	        self._executor = executor
   101	        self._prediction_store = prediction_store
   102	        self._result: ModelRefitResult | None = None
   103	        self._lock = threading.Lock()
   104	
   105	    def _execute_refit(self) -> ModelRefitResult:
   106	        """Execute the refit and return a ModelRefitResult.
   107	
   108	        Thread-safe: uses a lock to prevent concurrent refits.
   109	        """
   110	        with self._lock:
   111	            if self._result is not None:
   112	                return self._result
   113	
   114	            # Build a RefitConfig from the selection metadata
   115	            from nirs4all.pipeline.execution.refit.config_extractor import RefitConfig
   116	            from nirs4all.pipeline.execution.refit.executor import execute_simple_refit
   117	
   118	            refit_config = RefitConfig(
   119	                expanded_steps=self.selection.expanded_steps,
   120	                best_params=self.selection.best_params,
   121	                variant_index=self.selection.variant_index,
   122	                metric=self._refit_config.metric,
   123	                selection_score=self.selection.best_score,
   124	            )
   125	
   126	            # Create a fresh prediction store for capturing refit predictions
   127	            from nirs4all.data.predictions import Predictions
   128	
   129	            refit_predictions = Predictions()
   130	
   131	            try:
   132	                refit_result = execute_simple_refit(
   133	                    refit_config=refit_config,
   134	                    dataset=self._dataset,
   135	                    context=self._context,
   136	                    runtime_context=self._runtime_context,
   137	                    artifact_registry=self._artifact_registry,
   138	                    executor=self._executor,
   139	                    prediction_store=refit_predictions,
   140	                )
   141	            except Exception:
   142	                logger.warning(
   143	                    f"Lazy refit for model '{self.model_name}' failed. "
   144	                    f"Resources may have been destroyed."
   145	                )
   146	                # Return a minimal result with just the CV info
   147	                self._result = ModelRefitResult(
   148	                    model_name=self.model_name,
   149	                    cv_score=self.selection.best_score,
   150	                    metric=self._refit_config.metric,
   151	                )
   152	                return self._result
   153	
   154	            # Build ModelRefitResult from the refit output
   155	            final_entries = refit_predictions.iter_entries(fold_id="final")
   156	            final_entry = final_entries[0] if final_entries else {}
   157	
   158	            self._result = ModelRefitResult(
   159	                model_name=self.model_name,
   160	                final_entry=final_entry,
   161	                cv_entry={},
   162	                final_score=refit_result.test_score,
   163	                cv_score=self.selection.best_score,
   164	                metric=refit_result.metric,
   165	            )
   166	            return self._result
   167	
   168	    def _ensure_result(self) -> ModelRefitResult:
   169	        """Ensure the refit has been executed and return the result."""
   170	        if self._result is None:
   171	            return self._execute_refit()
   172	        return self._result
   173	
   174	    @property
   175	    def score(self) -> float | None:
   176	        """Get the refit model's test score (triggers refit on first access)."""
   177	        return self._ensure_result().final_score
   178	
   179	    @property
   180	    def final_score(self) -> float | None:
   181	        """Get the refit model's test score (triggers refit on first access)."""
   182	        return self._ensure_result().final_score
   183	
   184	    @property
   185	    def final_entry(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   186	        """Get the refit prediction entry (triggers refit on first access)."""
   187	        return self._ensure_result().final_entry
   188	
   189	    @property
   190	    def cv_entry(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   191	        """Get the best CV prediction entry."""
   192	        return self._ensure_result().cv_entry
   193	
   194	    @property
   195	    def cv_score(self) -> float | None:
   196	        """Get the best CV validation score (does not trigger refit)."""
   197	        return self.selection.best_score
   198	
   199	    @property
   200	    def metric(self) -> str:
   201	        """Get the metric name (does not trigger refit)."""
   202	        return self._refit_config.metric
   203	
   204	    @property
   205	    def is_resolved(self) -> bool:
   206	        """Check if the refit has already been executed."""
   207	        return self._result is not None
   208	
   209	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
   210	        status = "resolved" if self.is_resolved else "pending"
   211	        return f"LazyModelRefitResult(model='{self.model_name}', status={status})"
   212	
   213	@dataclass
   214	class RunResult:
   215	    """Result from nirs4all.run().
   216	
   217	    Provides convenient access to predictions, best model, and artifacts.
   218	    Wraps the raw (predictions, per_dataset) tuple returned by PipelineRunner.run().
   219	
   220	    Attributes:
   221	        predictions: Predictions object containing all pipeline results.
   222	        per_dataset: Dictionary with per-dataset execution details.
   223	
   224	    Properties:
   225	        best: Best prediction entry by default ranking.
   226	        best_score: Best model's primary test score (CV selection metric).
   227	        best_rmse: Best model's RMSE (regression).
   228	        best_r2: Best model's R² (regression).
   229	        best_accuracy: Best model's accuracy (classification).
   230	        final: Refit model prediction entry (``fold_id="final"``), or ``None``.
   231	        final_score: Refit model test score, or ``None`` if no refit.
   232	        cv_best: Best CV prediction entry.
   233	        cv_best_score: Best CV validation score.
   234	        models: Per-model refit results (for Phase 2, one entry).
   235	        artifacts_path: Path to run artifacts directory.
   236	        num_predictions: Total number of predictions stored.
   237	
   238	    Key Operations:
   239	        top(n): Get top N predictions by ranking.
   240	        export(path): Export best model to .n4a bundle.
   241	        filter(**kwargs): Filter predictions by criteria.
   242	        get_datasets(): Get list of unique dataset names.
   243	        get_models(): Get list of unique model names.
   244	
   245	    Example:
   246	        >>> result = nirs4all.run(pipeline, dataset)
   247	        >>> print(f"Best RMSE: {result.best_rmse:.4f}")
   248	        >>> print(f"Best R²: {result.best_r2:.4f}")
   249	        >>> result.export("exports/best_model.n4a")
   250	    """
   251	
   252	    predictions: Predictions
   253	    per_dataset: dict[str, Any]
   254	    _runner: PipelineRunner | None = field(default=None, repr=False)
   255	    _owns_runner: bool = field(default=True, repr=False)
   256	    _workspace_path: Path | None = field(default=None, repr=False)
   257	
   258	    # Lazy refit dependencies (set by the orchestrator when per-model
   259	    # selections are available so that ``models`` returns lazy results)
   260	    _per_model_selections: dict[str, PerModelSelection] | None = field(default=None, repr=False)
   261	    _refit_config: RefitConfig | None = field(default=None, repr=False)
   262	    _refit_dataset: Any = field(default=None, repr=False)
   263	    _refit_context: Any = field(default=None, repr=False)
   264	    _refit_runtime_context: Any = field(default=None, repr=False)
   265	    _refit_artifact_registry: Any = field(default=None, repr=False)
   266	    _refit_executor: Any = field(default=None, repr=False)
   267	
   268	    # --- Lifecycle ---
   269	
   270	    def detach(self) -> None:
   271	        """Detach from the runner by closing its store and dropping the reference.
   272	
   273	        After detaching, the RunResult operates in detached mode: export
   274	        operations re-open the store on demand.  This releases the DB
   275	        connection so other processes can access the workspace.
   276	
   277	        Called automatically by :func:`nirs4all.run` for non-session runs.
   278	        """
   279	        if self._runner is not None and self._owns_runner:
   280	            if self._workspace_path is None:
   281	                self._workspace_path = getattr(self._runner, 'workspace_path', None)
   282	            self._runner.close()
   283	            self._runner = None
   284	
   285	    def close(self) -> None:
   286	        """Close the underlying WorkspaceStore to release DB resources.
   287	
   288	        Safe to call multiple times.  For detached results this is a no-op.
   289	        Session-owned runners are closed by the session.
   290	        """
   291	        if self._runner is not None and self._owns_runner:
   292	            self._runner.close()
   293	
   294	    def __enter__(self) -> RunResult:
   295	        return self
   296	
   297	    def __exit__(self, *exc: object) -> None:
   298	        self.close()
   299	
   300	    def __del__(self) -> None:
   301	        """Safety net: close store if caller forgot."""
   302	        with contextlib.suppress(Exception):
   303	            self.close()
   304	
   305	    # --- Primary accessors ---
   306	
   307	    @property
   308	    def best(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   309	        """Get the best prediction entry, preferring refit (final) models.
   310	
   311	        When refit entries exist, returns the best final entry.
   312	        Otherwise falls back to the best CV entry.
   313	
   314	        Returns:
   315	            Dictionary containing best model's metrics, name, and configuration.
   316	            Empty dict if no predictions available.
   317	        """
   318	        final = self.best_final
   319	        if final:
   320	            return final
   321	        return self.cv_best
   322	
   323	    @property
   324	    def best_score(self) -> float:
   325	        """Get best model's primary test score.
   326	
   327	        Returns:
   328	            The test_score value from best prediction, or NaN if unavailable.
   329	        """
   330	        score = self.best.get('test_score')
   331	        return float(score) if score is not None else float('nan')
   332	
   333	    @property
   334	    def best_rmse(self) -> float:
   335	        """Get best model's RMSE score.
   336	
   337	        Looks for 'rmse' as a flat key (from display_metrics), then in scores dict,
   338	        then falls back to test_score if metric is rmse-like.
   339	
   340	        Returns:
   341	            RMSE value or NaN if unavailable.
   342	        """
   343	        entry = self.predictions.get_best(metric="rmse", task_type="regression", score_scope="all")
   344	        best = entry if entry else self.best
   345	        if not best:
   346	            return float('nan')
   347	
   348	        # Try flat 'rmse' key first (from display_metrics)
   349	        if 'rmse' in best and best['rmse'] is not None:
   350	            return float(best['rmse'])
   351	
   352	        # Try nested scores dict (legacy format)
   353	        scores = best.get('scores', {})
   354	        if isinstance(scores, dict):
   355	            test_scores = scores.get('test', {})
   356	            if 'rmse' in test_scores and test_scores['rmse'] is not None:
   357	                return float(test_scores['rmse'])
   358	
   359	        # Fall back to test_score if metric is rmse-like
   360	        metric = best.get('metric', '')
   361	        if metric in ('rmse', 'mse'):
   362	            test_score = best.get('test_score')
   363	            if test_score is not None:
   364	                return float(test_score)
   365	
   366	        return float('nan')
   367	
   368	    @property
   369	    def best_r2(self) -> float:
   370	        """Get best model's R² score.
   371	
   372	        Looks for 'r2' as a flat key (from display_metrics), then in scores dict.
   373	
   374	        Returns:
   375	            R² value or NaN if unavailable.
   376	        """
   377	        entry = self.predictions.get_best(metric="r2", task_type="regression", score_scope="all")
   378	        best = entry if entry else self.best
   379	        if not best:
   380	            return float('nan')
   381	
   382	        # Try flat 'r2' key first (from display_metrics)
   383	        if 'r2' in best and best['r2'] is not None:
   384	            return float(best['r2'])
   385	
   386	        # Try nested scores dict (legacy format)
   387	        scores = best.get('scores', {})
   388	        if isinstance(scores, dict):
   389	            test_scores = scores.get('test', {})
   390	            if 'r2' in test_scores and test_scores['r2'] is not None:
   391	                return float(test_scores['r2'])
   392	
   393	        return float('nan')
   394	
   395	    @property
   396	    def best_accuracy(self) -> float:
   397	        """Get best model's accuracy score (for classification).
   398	
   399	        Looks for 'accuracy' as a flat key (from display_metrics), then in scores dict.
   400	
   401	        Returns:
   402	            Accuracy value or NaN if unavailable.
   403	        """
   404	        entry = self.predictions.get_best(metric="accuracy", task_type="classification", score_scope="all")
   405	        best = entry if entry else self.best
   406	        if not best:
   407	            return float('nan')
   408	
   409	        # Try flat 'accuracy' key first (from display_metrics)
   410	        if 'accuracy' in best and best['accuracy'] is not None:
   411	            return float(best['accuracy'])
   412	
   413	        # Try nested scores dict (legacy format)
   414	        scores = best.get('scores', {})
   415	        if isinstance(scores, dict):
   416	            test_scores = scores.get('test', {})
   417	            if 'accuracy' in test_scores and test_scores['accuracy'] is not None:
   418	                return float(test_scores['accuracy'])
   419	
   420	        # Fall back to test_score if metric is accuracy
   421	        metric = best.get('metric', '')
   422	        if metric == 'accuracy':
   423	            test_score = best.get('test_score')
   424	            if test_score is not None:
   425	                return float(test_score)
   426	
   427	        return float('nan')
   428	
   429	    # --- Refit accessors ---
   430	
   431	    @property
   432	    def best_final(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   433	        """Get the best refit entry across all models.
   434	
   435	        Filters predictions to ``fold_id="final"`` entries and ranks them
   436	        by their selection score (``selection_score``).
   437	
   438	        Returns:
   439	            Best refit prediction dict, or empty dict if no refit entries.
   440	        """
   441	        results = self.predictions.top(n=1, score_scope="refit")
   442	        top = cast(list, results)
   443	        return top[0] if top else {}
   444	
   445	    @property
   446	    def final(self) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
   447	        """Get the refit model prediction entry (``fold_id="final"``).
   448	
   449	        Searches the per-dataset prediction stores where refit entries
   450	        are stored (they are not merged into the global predictions
   451	        buffer to avoid polluting CV-centric ranking).
   452	
   453	        Returns:
   454	            Prediction dict for the refit model, or ``None`` if refit
   455	            was not performed or no refit entries exist.
   456	        """
   457	        # Search per-dataset prediction stores (refit entries live here)
   458	        for ds_info in self.per_dataset.values():
   459	            ds_preds = ds_info.get("run_predictions")
   460	            if ds_preds is None:
   461	                continue
   462	            entries = ds_preds.filter_predictions(fold_id="final")
   463	            for entry in entries:
   464	                if str(entry.get("fold_id")) == "final":
   465	                    return dict(entry)
   466	        # Fallback: check global predictions (for backward compatibility)
   467	        entries = self.predictions.filter_predictions(fold_id="final")
   468	        for entry in entries:
   469	            if str(entry.get("fold_id")) == "final":
   470	                return dict(entry)
   471	        return None
   472	
   473	    @property
   474	    def final_score(self) -> float | None:
   475	        """Get the refit model's test score.
   476	
   477	        Returns:
   478	            Test score from the refit entry, or ``None`` if refit was
   479	            not performed.
   480	        """
   481	        entry = self.final
   482	        if entry is None:
   483	            return None
   484	        score = entry.get("test_score")
   485	        if score is not None:
   486	            return float(score)
   487	        return None
   488	
   489	    @property
   490	    def cv_best(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
   491	        """Get the best CV prediction entry (excludes refit entries).
   492	
   493	        This is the prediction entry that won the cross-validation
   494	        selection phase.  Refit entries (``fold_id="final"``) are
   495	        excluded from ranking.
   496	
   497	        Returns:
   498	            Best CV prediction dict, or empty dict if no CV predictions.
   499	        """
   500	        results = self.predictions.top(n=1, score_scope="folds", fold_id="avg")
   501	        top = cast(list[dict[str, Any]], results)
   502	        if top:
   503	            return top[0]
   504	
   505	        results = self.predictions.top(n=1, score_scope="folds")
   506	        top = cast(list[dict[str, Any]], results)
   507	        return top[0] if top else {}
   508	
   509	    @property
   510	    def cv_best_score(self) -> float:
   511	        """Get the best CV validation score.
   512	
   513	        Returns:
   514	            The val_score from the best CV entry, or NaN if unavailable.
   515	        """
   516	        entry = self.cv_best
   517	        if not entry:
   518	            return float("nan")
   519	        score = entry.get("val_score")
   520	        if score is not None:
   521	            return float(score)
   522	        return float("nan")
   523	
   524	    @property
   525	    def models(self) -> dict[str, ModelRefitResult | LazyModelRefitResult]:
   526	        """Get per-model refit results.
   527	
   528	        When per-model selections are available (set by the orchestrator),
   529	        returns :class:`LazyModelRefitResult` instances that defer the
   530	        actual refit until a property requiring the result is accessed.
   531	
   532	        When per-model selections are not available, falls back to
   533	        the eager approach using already-executed refit entries.
   534	
   535	        Returns:
   536	            Dictionary mapping model name to :class:`ModelRefitResult`
   537	            or :class:`LazyModelRefitResult`.
   538	        """
   539	        # Lazy path: per-model selections were stored by the orchestrator
   540	        if self._per_model_selections is not None and self._refit_config is not None:
   541	            result: dict[str, ModelRefitResult | LazyModelRefitResult] = {}
   542	            for model_name, selection in self._per_model_selections.items():
   543	                result[model_name] = LazyModelRefitResult(
   544	                    model_name=model_name,
   545	                    selection=selection,
   546	                    refit_config=self._refit_config,
   547	                    dataset=self._refit_dataset,
   548	                    context=self._refit_context,
   549	                    runtime_context=self._refit_runtime_context,
   550	                    artifact_registry=self._refit_artifact_registry,
   551	                    executor=self._refit_executor,
   552	                    prediction_store=self.predictions,
   553	                )
   554	            return result
   555	
   556	        # Eager fallback: use already-executed refit entries
   557	        final_entry = self.final
   558	        if final_entry is None:
   559	            return {}
   560	
   561	        model_name = final_entry.get("model_name", "unknown")
   562	        cv_entry = self.cv_best
   563	        metric = final_entry.get("metric", "")
   564	
   565	        final_score_val = final_entry.get("test_score")
   566	        cv_score_val = cv_entry.get("val_score") if cv_entry else None
   567	
   568	        return {
   569	            model_name: ModelRefitResult(
   570	                model_name=model_name,
   571	                final_entry=final_entry,
   572	                cv_entry=cv_entry,
   573	                final_score=float(final_score_val) if final_score_val is not None else None,
   574	                cv_score=float(cv_score_val) if cv_score_val is not None else None,
   575	                metric=metric,
   576	            )
   577	        }
   578	
   579	    # --- Metadata accessors ---
   580	
   581	    @property
   582	    def artifacts_path(self) -> Path | None:
   583	        """Get path to workspace artifacts directory.
   584	
   585	        Returns:
   586	            Path to the workspace directory, or None if not available.
   587	        """
   588	        if self._workspace_path is not None:
   589	            return self._workspace_path
   590	        if self._runner and hasattr(self._runner, 'workspace_path'):
   591	            return self._runner.workspace_path
   592	        return None
   593	
   594	    @property
   595	    def num_predictions(self) -> int:
   596	        """Get total number of predictions stored.
   597	
   598	        Returns:
   599	            Number of prediction entries.
   600	        """
   601	        return self.predictions.num_predictions
   602	
   603	    # --- Query methods ---
   604	
   605	    def top(self, n: int = 5, **kwargs) -> Any:
   606	        """Get top N predictions by ranking.
   607	
   608	        Args:
   609	            n: Number of top predictions to return. When group_by is used,
   610	               this means top N **per group** (e.g., top 3 per dataset).
   611	            **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to predictions.top().
   612	                Supported kwargs include:
   613	                - rank_metric: Metric to rank by (default: uses record's metric)
   614	                - rank_partition: Partition to rank on (default: "val")
   615	                - display_partition: Partition for display metrics (default: "test")
   616	                - aggregate_partitions: If True, include train/val/test data
   617	                - ascending: Sort order (None = infer from metric)
   618	                - group_by: Group predictions by column(s). Returns top N per group.
   619	                  Each result includes 'group_key' for easy filtering.
   620	                - return_grouped: If True with group_by, return dict of group->results
   621	                  instead of flat list. Default: False.
   622	
   623	        Returns:
   624	            - If return_grouped=False (default): List of prediction dicts,
   625	              ranked by score. With group_by, returns top N per group as flat list.
   626	            - If return_grouped=True: Dict mapping group keys to lists of predictions.
   627	
   628	        Examples:
   629	            >>> # Top 5 overall
   630	            >>> result.top(5)
   631	            >>>
   632	            >>> # Top 3 per dataset (flat list)
   633	            >>> top_per_ds = result.top(3, group_by='dataset_name')
   634	            >>> ds1 = [r for r in top_per_ds if r['group_key'] == ('my_dataset',)]
   635	            >>>
   636	            >>> # Top 3 per dataset (grouped dict)
   637	            >>> grouped = result.top(3, group_by='dataset_name', return_grouped=True)
   638	            >>> for key, results in grouped.items():
   639	            ...     print(f"{key}: {len(results)} results")
   640	            >>>
   641	            >>> # Multi-column grouping: top 2 per (dataset, model) combination
   642	            >>> top_per_combo = result.top(2, group_by=['dataset_name', 'model_name'])
   643	            >>> # Group keys are tuples: ('wheat', 'PLSRegression'), ('corn', 'RandomForest')
   644	            >>> for r in top_per_combo:
   645	            ...     dataset, model = r['group_key']
   646	            ...     print(f"{dataset}/{model}: {r['test_score']:.4f}")
   647	        """
   648	        return self.predictions.top(n=n, **kwargs)
   649	
   650	    def filter(self, **kwargs) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   651	        """Filter predictions by criteria.
   652	
   653	        Args:
   654	            **kwargs: Filter criteria passed to predictions.filter_predictions().
   655	                Supported kwargs include:
   656	                - dataset_name: Filter by dataset name
   657	                - model_name: Filter by model name
   658	                - partition: Filter by partition ('train', 'val', 'test')
   659	                - fold_id: Filter by fold ID
   660	                - step_idx: Filter by pipeline step index
   661	                - branch_id: Filter by branch ID
   662	                - load_arrays: If True, load actual arrays (default: True)
   663	
   664	        Returns:
   665	            List of matching prediction dictionaries.
   666	        """
   667	        return self.predictions.filter_predictions(**kwargs)
   668	
   669	    def get_datasets(self) -> list[str]:
   670	        """Get list of unique dataset names.
   671	
   672	        Returns:
   673	            List of dataset names in predictions.
   674	        """
   675	        return self.predictions.get_datasets()
   676	
   677	    def get_models(self) -> list[str]:
   678	        """Get list of unique model names.
   679	
   680	        Returns:
   681	            List of model names in predictions.
   682	        """
   683	        return self.predictions.get_models()
   684	
   685	    # --- Export methods ---
   686	
   687	    def _open_store_for_export(self):
   688	        """Open a temporary WorkspaceStore for export operations.
   689	
   690	        Returns a context-managed store that is closed after use.
   691	        Works in both attached (runner alive) and detached modes.
   692	        """
   693	        # Attached mode: use runner's store directly
   694	        if self._runner is not None:
   695	            return contextlib.nullcontext(self._runner.store)
   696	
   697	        # Detached mode: open a fresh store
   698	        if self._workspace_path is None:
   699	            raise RuntimeError("Cannot export: no workspace path available (result was not created from a workspace run)")
   700	
   701	        from nirs4all.pipeline.storage.workspace_store import WorkspaceStore
   702	
   703	        class _TempStore:
   704	            def __init__(self, path: Path):
   705	                self._store = WorkspaceStore(path)
   706	
   707	            def __enter__(self):
   708	                return self._store
   709	
   710	            def __exit__(self, *exc: object):
   711	                self._store.close()
   712	
   713	        return _TempStore(self._workspace_path)
   714	
   715	    def export(
   716	        self,
   717	        output_path: str | Path,
   718	        format: str = "n4a",
   719	        source: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
   720	        chain_id: str | None = None,
   721	    ) -> Path:
   722	        """Export a model to bundle.
   723	
   724	        Two export paths are supported:
   725	
   726	        **Store-based** (preferred) -- pass ``chain_id`` to export
   727	        directly from the workspace store:
   728	
   729	        >>> result.export("model.n4a", chain_id="abc123")
   730	
   731	        **Resolver-based** -- exports via ``BundleGenerator``:
   732	
   733	        >>> result.export("model.n4a")  # uses best prediction
   734	
   735	        Works in both attached (runner alive) and detached modes.
   736	        In detached mode, a temporary store is opened for the export
   737	        and closed immediately after.
   738	
   739	        Args:
   740	            output_path: Path for the exported bundle file.
   741	            format: Export format ('n4a' or 'n4a.py').
   742	            source: Prediction dict to export. If None, exports best model.
   743	            chain_id: Chain identifier for store-based export.
   744	                When provided, ``source`` is ignored and the chain is
   745	                exported directly from the workspace store.
   746	
   747	        Returns:
   748	            Path to the exported bundle file.
   749	
   750	        Raises:
   751	            RuntimeError: If no workspace path available.
   752	            ValueError: If no predictions available and source not provided.
   753	        """
   754	        # Store-based export path
   755	        if chain_id is not None:
   756	            with self._open_store_for_export() as store:
   757	                if store is None:
   758	                    raise RuntimeError("Cannot export from chain_id: no WorkspaceStore available")
   759	                return Path(store.export_chain(chain_id, Path(output_path), format=format))
   760	
   761	        # Resolver-based path
   762	        if source is None:
   763	            source = self.final or self.best
   764	            if not source:
   765	                raise ValueError("No predictions available to export")
   766	
   767	        # Attached mode: delegate to runner
   768	        if self._runner is not None:
   769	            return Path(self._runner.export(source=source, output_path=output_path, format=format))
   770	
   771	        # Detached mode: create BundleGenerator with temporary store
   772	        workspace_path = self._workspace_path
   773	        if workspace_path is None:
   774	            raise RuntimeError("Cannot export: no workspace path available")
   775	
   776	        from nirs4all.pipeline.bundle import BundleGenerator
   777	
   778	        with self._open_store_for_export() as store:
   779	            generator = BundleGenerator(workspace_path=workspace_path, verbose=0, store=store)
   780	            return generator.export(source=source, output_path=output_path, format=format)
   781	
   782	    def export_model(
   783	        self,
   784	        output_path: str | Path,
   785	        source: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
   786	        format: str | None = None,
   787	        fold: int | None = None
   788	    ) -> Path:
   789	        """Export only the model artifact (lightweight).
   790	
   791	        Unlike export() which creates a full bundle, this exports just the model.
   792	        Works in both attached (runner alive) and detached modes.
   793	
   794	        Args:
   795	            output_path: Path for the output model file.
   796	            source: Prediction dict to export. If None, exports best model.
   797	            format: Model format (inferred from extension if None).
   798	            fold: Fold index to export (default: fold 0).
   799	
   800	        Returns:
   801	            Path to the exported model file.
   802	
   803	        Raises:
   804	            RuntimeError: If no workspace path available.
   805	        """
   806	        if source is None:
   807	            source = self.best
   808	            if not source:
   809	                raise ValueError("No predictions available to export")
   810	
   811	        # Attached mode: delegate to runner
   812	        if self._runner is not None:
   813	            return self._runner.export_model(source=source, output_path=output_path, format=format, fold=fold)
   814	
   815	        # Detached mode: replicate runner.export_model logic with temporary store
   816	        workspace_path = self._workspace_path
   817	        if workspace_path is None:
   818	            raise RuntimeError("Cannot export: no workspace path available")
   819	
   820	        from nirs4all.pipeline.resolver import PredictionResolver
   821	        from nirs4all.pipeline.storage.artifacts.artifact_persistence import to_bytes
   822	
   823	        output_path = Path(output_path)
   824	        output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   825	
   826	        with self._open_store_for_export() as store:
   827	            resolver = PredictionResolver(workspace_path=workspace_path, runs_dir=workspace_path, store=store)
   828	            resolved = resolver.resolve(source, verbose=0)
   829	
   830	            if resolved.model_step_index is None:
   831	                raise ValueError("No model step found in the resolved prediction")
   832	            if resolved.artifact_provider is None:
   833	                raise ValueError("No artifact provider available for this source")
   834	
   835	            artifacts = resolved.artifact_provider.get_artifacts_for_step(resolved.model_step_index)
   836	            if not artifacts:
   837	                raise ValueError(f"No model artifacts found at step {resolved.model_step_index}")
   838	
   839	            if fold is not None:
   840	                model = None
   841	                for artifact_id, artifact in artifacts:
   842	                    if f":{fold}" in str(artifact_id) or artifact_id.endswith(f"_{fold}"):
   843	                        model = artifact
   844	                        break
   845	                if model is None:
   846	                    raise ValueError(f"No artifact found for fold {fold}")
   847	            else:
   848	                _, model = artifacts[0]
   849	
   850	        if format is None:
   851	            ext = output_path.suffix.lower()
   852	            format_map = {'.joblib': 'joblib', '.pkl': 'cloudpickle', '.pickle': 'cloudpickle', '.h5': 'keras_h5', '.hdf5': 'keras_h5', '.keras': 'tensorflow_keras', '.pt': 'pytorch_state_dict', '.pth': 'pytorch_state_dict'}
   853	            format = format_map.get(ext, 'joblib')
   854	
   855	        data, _actual_format = to_bytes(model, format)
   856	        with open(output_path, 'wb') as f:
   857	            f.write(data)
   858	
   859	        return output_path
   860	
   861	    # --- Utility methods ---
   862	
   863	    def summary(self) -> str:
   864	        """Get a summary string of the run result.
   865	
   866	        Returns:
   867	            Multi-line summary string with key metrics.
   868	        """
   869	        lines = []
   870	        lines.append(f"RunResult: {self.num_predictions} predictions")
   871	
   872	        if self.artifacts_path:
   873	            lines.append(f"  Artifacts: {self.artifacts_path}")
   874	
   875	        datasets = self.get_datasets()
   876	        if datasets:
   877	            lines.append(f"  Datasets: {', '.join(datasets)}")
   878	
   879	        models = self.get_models()
   880	        if models:
   881	            lines.append(f"  Models: {', '.join(models[:5])}" +
   882	                        (f" (+{len(models)-5} more)" if len(models) > 5 else ""))
   883	
   884	        best = self.best
   885	        if best:
   886	            lines.append(f"  Best: {best.get('model_name', 'unknown')}")
   887	            lines.append(f"    test_score: {self.best_score:.4f}")
   888	            if not np.isnan(self.best_rmse):
   889	                lines.append(f"    rmse: {self.best_rmse:.4f}")
   890	            if not np.isnan(self.best_r2):
   891	                lines.append(f"    r2: {self.best_r2:.4f}")
   892	
   893	        return "\n".join(lines)
   894	
   895	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
   896	        """String representation."""
   897	        return f"RunResult(predictions={self.num_predictions}, best_score={self.best_score:.4f})"
   898	
   899	    def __str__(self) -> str:
   900	        """User-friendly string representation."""
   901	        return self.summary()
   902	
   903	    def validate(
   904	        self,
   905	        check_nan_metrics: bool = True,
   906	        check_empty: bool = True,
   907	        raise_on_failure: bool = True,
   908	        nan_threshold: float = 0.0
   909	    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
   910	        """Validate the run result for common issues.
   911	
   912	        Checks for NaN values in metrics, empty predictions, and other issues
   913	        that might indicate problems with the pipeline execution.
   914	
   915	        Args:
   916	            check_nan_metrics: If True, check for NaN values in metrics.
   917	            check_empty: If True, check for empty predictions.
   918	            raise_on_failure: If True, raise ValueError on validation failure.
   919	            nan_threshold: Maximum allowed ratio of predictions with NaN metrics (0.0 = none allowed).
   920	
   921	        Returns:
   922	            Dictionary with validation results:
   923	                - valid: True if all checks passed.
   924	                - issues: List of issue descriptions.
   925	                - nan_count: Number of predictions with NaN metrics.
   926	                - total_count: Total number of predictions.
   927	
   928	        Raises:
   929	            ValueError: If raise_on_failure=True and validation fails.
   930	
   931	        Example:
   932	            >>> result = nirs4all.run(pipeline, dataset)
   933	            >>> result.validate()  # Raises if issues found
   934	            >>> # Or check without raising
   935	            >>> report = result.validate(raise_on_failure=False)
   936	            >>> if not report['valid']:
   937	            ...     print(f"Issues: {report['issues']}")
   938	        """
   939	        issues = []
   940	        nan_count = 0
   941	        total_count = self.num_predictions
   942	
   943	        # Check for empty predictions
   944	        if check_empty and total_count == 0:
   945	            issues.append("No predictions found")
   946	
   947	        # Check for NaN metrics
   948	        if check_nan_metrics and total_count > 0:
   949	            all_preds = self.predictions.filter_predictions(load_arrays=False)
   950	            for pred in all_preds:
   951	                has_nan = False
   952	                # Check common metrics
   953	                for metric in ['rmse', 'r2', 'accuracy', 'mse', 'mae']:
   954	                    value = pred.get(metric)
   955	                    if value is not None and np.isnan(value):
   956	                        has_nan = True
   957	                        break
   958	
   959	                # Check scores dict
   960	                if not has_nan:
   961	                    scores = pred.get('scores', {})
   962	                    if isinstance(scores, dict):
   963	                        for partition_scores in scores.values():
   964	                            if isinstance(partition_scores, dict):
   965	                                for val in partition_scores.values():
   966	                                    if isinstance(val, (int, float)) and np.isnan(val):
   967	                                        has_nan = True
   968	                                        break
   969	
   970	                # Check score fields
   971	                if not has_nan:
   972	                    for score_key in ('test_score', 'val_score', 'train_score'):
   973	                        score_val = pred.get(score_key)
   974	                        if score_val is not None and isinstance(score_val, float) and np.isnan(score_val):
   975	                            has_nan = True
   976	                            break
   977	
   978	                if has_nan:
   979	                    nan_count += 1
   980	
   981	            # Check threshold
   982	            if nan_count > 0:
   983	                nan_ratio = nan_count / total_count if total_count > 0 else 0
   984	                if nan_ratio > nan_threshold:
   985	                    issues.append(
   986	                        f"NaN ratio ({nan_ratio:.1%}) exceeds threshold ({nan_threshold:.1%}): "
   987	                        f"{nan_count} of {total_count} predictions have NaN metrics"
   988	                    )
   989	
   990	        valid = len(issues) == 0
   991	
   992	        report = {
   993	            'valid': valid,
   994	            'issues': issues,
   995	            'nan_count': nan_count,
   996	            'total_count': total_count,
   997	        }
   998	
   999	        if raise_on_failure and not valid:
  1000	            raise ValueError(
  1001	                "RunResult validation failed:\n" +
  1002	                "\n".join(f"  - {issue}" for issue in issues)
  1003	            )
  1004	
  1005	        return report
  1006	
  1007	@dataclass
  1008	class PredictResult:
  1009	    """Result from nirs4all.predict().
  1010	
  1011	    Wraps prediction outputs with convenient accessors and conversion methods.
  1012	
  1013	    Attributes:
  1014	        y_pred: Predicted values array (n_samples,) or (n_samples, n_outputs).
  1015	        metadata: Additional prediction metadata (uncertainty, timing, etc.).
  1016	        sample_indices: Optional indices of predicted samples.
  1017	        model_name: Name of the model used for prediction.
  1018	        preprocessing_steps: List of preprocessing steps applied.
  1019	
  1020	    Properties:
  1021	        values: Alias for y_pred (for consistency).
  1022	        shape: Shape of prediction array.
  1023	        is_multioutput: True if predictions have multiple outputs.
  1024	
  1025	    Key Operations:
  1026	        to_numpy(): Get predictions as numpy array.
  1027	        to_list(): Get predictions as Python list.
  1028	        to_dataframe(): Get predictions as pandas DataFrame.
  1029	        flatten(): Get flattened 1D predictions.
  1030	
  1031	    Example:
  1032	        >>> result = nirs4all.predict(model, X_new)
  1033	        >>> print(f"Predictions shape: {result.shape}")
  1034	        >>> df = result.to_dataframe()
  1035	    """
  1036	
  1037	    y_pred: np.ndarray
  1038	    metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
  1039	    sample_indices: np.ndarray | None = None
  1040	    model_name: str = ""
  1041	    preprocessing_steps: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
  1042	
  1043	    def __post_init__(self):
  1044	        """Ensure y_pred is a numpy array."""
  1045	        if self.y_pred is not None and not isinstance(self.y_pred, np.ndarray):
  1046	            self.y_pred = np.asarray(self.y_pred)
  1047	
  1048	    @property
  1049	    def values(self) -> np.ndarray:
  1050	        """Get prediction values (alias for y_pred)."""
  1051	        return self.y_pred
  1052	
  1053	    @property
  1054	    def shape(self) -> tuple:
  1055	        """Get shape of prediction array."""
  1056	        if self.y_pred is None:
  1057	            return (0,)
  1058	        return self.y_pred.shape
  1059	
  1060	    @property
  1061	    def is_multioutput(self) -> bool:
  1062	        """Check if predictions have multiple outputs."""
  1063	        return len(self.shape) > 1 and self.shape[1] > 1
  1064	
  1065	    def __len__(self) -> int:
  1066	        """Return number of predictions."""
  1067	        if self.y_pred is None:
  1068	            return 0
  1069	        return len(self.y_pred)
  1070	
  1071	    def to_numpy(self) -> np.ndarray:
  1072	        """Get predictions as numpy array.
  1073	
  1074	        Returns:
  1075	            Numpy array of predictions.
  1076	        """
  1077	        return self.y_pred
  1078	
  1079	    def to_list(self) -> list[float]:
  1080	        """Get predictions as Python list.
  1081	
  1082	        Returns:
  1083	            List of prediction values (flattened if 2D).
  1084	        """
  1085	        if self.y_pred is None:
  1086	            return []
  1087	        return self.y_pred.flatten().tolist()
  1088	
  1089	    def to_dataframe(self, include_indices: bool = True):
  1090	        """Get predictions as pandas DataFrame.
  1091	
  1092	        Args:
  1093	            include_indices: If True and sample_indices available, include as column.
  1094	
  1095	        Returns:
  1096	            pandas DataFrame with predictions.
  1097	
  1098	        Raises:
  1099	            ImportError: If pandas is not available.
  1100	        """
  1101	        try:
  1102	            import pandas as pd
  1103	        except ImportError as err:
  1104	            raise ImportError("pandas is required for to_dataframe()") from err
  1105	
  1106	        data = {}
  1107	
  1108	        if include_indices and self.sample_indices is not None:
  1109	            data['sample_index'] = self.sample_indices
  1110	
  1111	        if self.is_multioutput:
  1112	            for i in range(self.shape[1]):
  1113	                data[f'y_pred_{i}'] = self.y_pred[:, i]
  1114	        else:
  1115	            data['y_pred'] = self.y_pred.flatten()
  1116	
  1117	        return pd.DataFrame(data)
  1118	
  1119	    def flatten(self) -> np.ndarray:
  1120	        """Get flattened 1D predictions.
  1121	
  1122	        Returns:
  1123	            1D numpy array of predictions.
  1124	        """
  1125	        if self.y_pred is None:
  1126	            return np.array([])
  1127	        return self.y_pred.flatten()
  1128	
  1129	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
  1130	        """String representation."""
  1131	        return f"PredictResult(shape={self.shape}, model='{self.model_name}')"
  1132	
  1133	    def __str__(self) -> str:
  1134	        """User-friendly string representation."""
  1135	        lines = [f"PredictResult: {len(self)} predictions"]
  1136	        if self.model_name:
  1137	            lines.append(f"  Model: {self.model_name}")
  1138	        if self.preprocessing_steps:
  1139	            lines.append(f"  Preprocessing: {' -> '.join(self.preprocessing_steps)}")
  1140	        lines.append(f"  Shape: {self.shape}")
  1141	        return "\n".join(lines)
  1142	
  1143	@dataclass
  1144	class ExplainResult:
  1145	    """Result from nirs4all.explain().
  1146	
  1147	    Wraps SHAP explanation outputs with visualization helpers and accessors.
  1148	
  1149	    Attributes:
  1150	        shap_values: SHAP values array or Explanation object.
  1151	        feature_names: Names/labels of features explained.
  1152	        base_value: Expected value (baseline prediction).
  1153	        visualizations: Paths to generated visualization files.
  1154	        explainer_type: Type of SHAP explainer used.
  1155	        model_name: Name of the explained model.
  1156	        n_samples: Number of samples explained.
  1157	
  1158	    Properties:
  1159	        values: Raw SHAP values array.
  1160	        shape: Shape of SHAP values array.
  1161	        mean_abs_shap: Mean absolute SHAP values per feature.
  1162	        top_features: Feature names sorted by importance.
  1163	
  1164	    Key Operations:
  1165	        get_feature_importance(): Get feature importance ranking.
  1166	        get_sample_explanation(idx): Get explanation for a single sample.
  1167	        to_dataframe(): Get SHAP values as DataFrame.
  1168	
  1169	    Example:
  1170	        >>> result = nirs4all.explain(model, X_test)
  1171	        >>> print(f"Top features: {result.top_features[:5]}")
  1172	        >>> importance = result.get_feature_importance()
  1173	    """
  1174	
  1175	    shap_values: Any  # shap.Explanation or np.ndarray
  1176	    feature_names: list[str] | None = None
  1177	    base_value: float | np.ndarray | None = None
  1178	    visualizations: dict[str, Path] = field(default_factory=dict)
  1179	    explainer_type: str = "auto"
  1180	    model_name: str = ""
  1181	    n_samples: int = 0
  1182	
  1183	    def __post_init__(self):
  1184	        """Extract metadata from shap_values if available."""
  1185	        if hasattr(self.shap_values, 'values'):
  1186	            # It's a shap.Explanation object
  1187	            if self.feature_names is None and hasattr(self.shap_values, 'feature_names'):
  1188	                self.feature_names = list(self.shap_values.feature_names)
  1189	            if self.base_value is None and hasattr(self.shap_values, 'base_values'):
  1190	                self.base_value = self.shap_values.base_values
  1191	            if self.n_samples == 0:
  1192	                self.n_samples = len(self.shap_values.values)
  1193	
  1194	    @property
  1195	    def values(self) -> np.ndarray:
  1196	        """Get raw SHAP values array.
  1197	
  1198	        Returns:
  1199	            Numpy array of SHAP values (n_samples, n_features).
  1200	        """
  1201	        if hasattr(self.shap_values, 'values'):
  1202	            return np.asarray(self.shap_values.values)
  1203	        return np.asarray(self.shap_values)
  1204	
  1205	    @property
  1206	    def shape(self) -> tuple:
  1207	        """Get shape of SHAP values array."""
  1208	        return self.values.shape
  1209	
  1210	    @property
  1211	    def mean_abs_shap(self) -> np.ndarray:
  1212	        """Get mean absolute SHAP values per feature.
  1213	
  1214	        Returns:
  1215	            1D array of mean |SHAP| values, one per feature.
  1216	        """
  1217	        vals = self.values
  1218	        if vals.ndim == 1:
  1219	            return np.asarray(np.abs(vals))
  1220	        return np.asarray(np.mean(np.abs(vals), axis=0))
  1221	
  1222	    @property
  1223	    def top_features(self) -> list[str]:
  1224	        """Get feature names sorted by importance (descending).
  1225	
  1226	        Returns:
  1227	            List of feature names, most important first.
  1228	            Returns indices as strings if feature_names not available.
  1229	        """
  1230	        importance = self.mean_abs_shap
  1231	        sorted_indices = np.argsort(importance)[::-1]
  1232	
  1233	        if self.feature_names:
  1234	            return [self.feature_names[i] for i in sorted_indices]
  1235	        return [str(i) for i in sorted_indices]
  1236	
  1237	    def get_feature_importance(
  1238	        self,
  1239	        top_n: int | None = None,
  1240	        normalize: bool = False
  1241	    ) -> dict[str, float]:
  1242	        """Get feature importance ranking.
  1243	
  1244	        Args:
  1245	            top_n: If provided, return only top N features.
  1246	            normalize: If True, normalize values to sum to 1.
  1247	
  1248	        Returns:
  1249	            Dictionary mapping feature names to importance values.
  1250	        """
  1251	        importance = self.mean_abs_shap
  1252	
  1253	        if normalize and importance.sum() > 0:
  1254	            importance = importance / importance.sum()
  1255	
  1256	        sorted_indices = np.argsort(importance)[::-1]
  1257	
  1258	        if top_n:
  1259	            sorted_indices = sorted_indices[:top_n]
  1260	
  1261	        result = {}
  1262	        for idx in sorted_indices:
  1263	            name = self.feature_names[idx] if self.feature_names else str(idx)
  1264	            result[name] = float(importance[idx])
  1265	
  1266	        return result
  1267	
  1268	    def get_sample_explanation(
  1269	        self,
  1270	        idx: int
  1271	    ) -> dict[str, float]:
  1272	        """Get SHAP explanation for a single sample.
  1273	
  1274	        Args:
  1275	            idx: Sample index.
  1276	
  1277	        Returns:
  1278	            Dictionary mapping feature names to SHAP values for that sample.
  1279	        """
  1280	        vals = self.values
  1281	        if idx >= len(vals):
  1282	            raise IndexError(f"Sample index {idx} out of range (n_samples={len(vals)})")
  1283	
  1284	        sample_shap = vals[idx] if vals.ndim > 1 else vals
  1285	
  1286	        result = {}
  1287	        for i, val in enumerate(sample_shap):
  1288	            name = self.feature_names[i] if self.feature_names else str(i)
  1289	            result[name] = float(val)
  1290	
  1291	        return result
  1292	
  1293	    def to_dataframe(self, include_feature_names: bool = True):
  1294	        """Get SHAP values as pandas DataFrame.
  1295	
  1296	        Args:
  1297	            include_feature_names: If True, use feature names as columns.
  1298	
  1299	        Returns:
  1300	            pandas DataFrame with SHAP values.
  1301	
  1302	        Raises:
  1303	            ImportError: If pandas is not available.
  1304	        """
  1305	        try:
  1306	            import pandas as pd
  1307	        except ImportError as err:
  1308	            raise ImportError("pandas is required for to_dataframe()") from err
  1309	
  1310	        vals = self.values
  1311	
  1312	        columns = self.feature_names if include_feature_names and self.feature_names else [f"feature_{i}" for i in range(vals.shape[-1])]
  1313	
  1314	        if vals.ndim == 1:
  1315	            vals = vals.reshape(1, -1)
  1316	
  1317	        return pd.DataFrame(vals, columns=columns)
  1318	
  1319	    def __repr__(self) -> str:
  1320	        """String representation."""
  1321	        return f"ExplainResult(shape={self.shape}, explainer='{self.explainer_type}')"
  1322	
  1323	    def __str__(self) -> str:
  1324	        """User-friendly string representation."""
  1325	        lines = [f"ExplainResult: {self.n_samples} samples explained"]
  1326	        if self.model_name:
  1327	            lines.append(f"  Model: {self.model_name}")
  1328	        lines.append(f"  Explainer: {self.explainer_type}")
  1329	        lines.append(f"  Shape: {self.shape}")
  1330	        if self.feature_names:
  1331	            lines.append(f"  Features: {len(self.feature_names)}")
  1332	
  1333	        # Show top 5 features
  1334	        top = self.top_features[:5]
  1335	        if top:
  1336	            lines.append(f"  Top features: {', '.join(top)}")
  1337	
  1338	        if self.visualizations:
  1339	            lines.append(f"  Visualizations: {list(self.visualizations.keys())}")
  1340	
  1341	        return "\n".join(lines)

/bin/bash -lc 'nl -ba nirs4all/pipeline/steps/parser.py' in /home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Step parser for pipeline step configurations."""
     2	from dataclasses import dataclass
     3	from enum import Enum
     4	from typing import Any, Optional
     5	
     6	from nirs4all.pipeline.config.component_serialization import deserialize_component
     7	
     8	
     9	class StepType(Enum):
    10	    """Types of pipeline steps."""
    11	    WORKFLOW = "workflow"  # model, preprocessing, chart, etc.
    12	    SERIALIZED = "serialized"  # class, function, module, etc.
    13	    SUBPIPELINE = "subpipeline"  # nested list of steps
    14	    DIRECT = "direct"  # direct operator instance
    15	    UNKNOWN = "unknown"
    16	
    17	@dataclass
    18	class ParsedStep:
    19	    """Normalized step configuration after parsing.
    20	
    21	    Attributes:
    22	        operator: Deserialized operator instance (or None for workflow ops)
    23	        keyword: Step keyword (e.g., 'model', 'preprocessing')
    24	        step_type: Type of step (workflow, serialized, etc.)
    25	        original_step: Original step configuration
    26	        metadata: Additional parsing metadata
    27	        force_layout: Optional forced data layout (overrides controller's preferred layout)
    28	    """
    29	    operator: Any
    30	    keyword: str
    31	    step_type: StepType
    32	    original_step: Any
    33	    metadata: dict[str, Any]
    34	    force_layout: str | None = None
    35	
    36	class StepParser:
    37	    """Parses pipeline step configurations into normalized format.
    38	
    39	    Handles multiple step syntaxes:
    40	    - Dictionary: {"model": SVC, "params": {...}}
    41	    - String: "sklearn.preprocessing.StandardScaler"
    42	    - Direct instance: StandardScaler()
    43	    - Nested lists: [[step1, step2], step3]
    44	
    45	    Normalizes to canonical ParsedStep format for controller execution.
    46	    """
    47	
    48	    # Known serialization operators
    49	    SERIALIZATION_OPERATORS = ["class", "function", "module", "object", "pipeline", "instance"]
    50	
    51	    # Reserved keywords that are not operators
    52	    RESERVED_KEYWORDS = ["params", "metadata", "steps", "name", "finetune_params", "train_params", "refit_params", "fit_on_all", "force_layout", "na_policy", "fill_value"]
    53	
    54	    # Valid layout values for force_layout
    55	    VALID_LAYOUTS = {"2d", "2d_interleaved", "3d", "3d_transpose"}
    56	
    57	    # Priority workflow keywords (ordered by priority, highest first)
    58	    WORKFLOW_KEYWORDS = [
    59	        "model",
    60	        "preprocessing",
    61	        "feature_augmentation",
    62	        "auto_transfer_preproc",
    63	        "concat_transform",
    64	        "y_processing",
    65	        "sample_augmentation",
    66	        "branch",
    67	    ]
    68	
    69	    def parse(self, step: Any) -> ParsedStep:
    70	        """Parse a pipeline step into normalized format.
    71	
    72	        Args:
    73	            step: Raw step configuration
    74	
    75	        Returns:
    76	            ParsedStep with normalized operator and metadata
    77	
    78	        Raises:
    79	            ValueError: If step format is invalid
    80	        """
    81	        if step is None:
    82	            return ParsedStep(
    83	                operator=None,
    84	                keyword="",
    85	                step_type=StepType.UNKNOWN,
    86	                original_step=step,
    87	                metadata={"skip": True}
    88	            )
    89	
    90	        # Handle MinimalPipelineStep (from trace extractor)
    91	        from nirs4all.pipeline.trace.extractor import MinimalPipelineStep
    92	        if isinstance(step, MinimalPipelineStep):
    93	            # Extract the step_config and parse it
    94	            return self.parse(step.step_config)
    95	
    96	        # Handle dictionary steps
    97	        if isinstance(step, dict):
    98	            return self._parse_dict_step(step)
    99	
   100	        # Handle list steps (subpipelines)
   101	        if isinstance(step, list):
   102	            return ParsedStep(
   103	                operator=None,
   104	                keyword="",
   105	                step_type=StepType.SUBPIPELINE,
   106	                original_step=step,
   107	                metadata={"steps": step}
   108	            )
   109	
   110	        # Handle string steps
   111	        if isinstance(step, str):
   112	            return self._parse_string_step(step)
   113	
   114	        # Handle direct operator instances
   115	        return ParsedStep(
   116	            operator=step,
   117	            keyword="",
   118	            step_type=StepType.DIRECT,
   119	            original_step=step,
   120	            metadata={}
   121	        )
   122	
   123	    def _parse_dict_step(self, step: dict[str, Any]) -> ParsedStep:
   124	        """Parse dictionary step configuration."""
   125	        # Extract and validate force_layout if present
   126	        force_layout = step.get("force_layout")
   127	        if force_layout is not None and force_layout not in self.VALID_LAYOUTS:
   128	            raise ValueError(
   129	                f"Invalid force_layout '{force_layout}'. "
   130	                f"Valid options: {self.VALID_LAYOUTS}"
   131	            )
   132	
   133	        # Check for serialization operators first
   134	        for key in self.SERIALIZATION_OPERATORS:
   135	            if key in step:
   136	                operator = deserialize_component(step)
   137	                return ParsedStep(
   138	                    operator=operator,
   139	                    keyword=key,
   140	                    step_type=StepType.SERIALIZED,
   141	                    original_step=step,
   142	                    metadata={},
   143	                    force_layout=force_layout
   144	                )
   145	
   146	        # Look for potential workflow operators
   147	        # Prioritize known workflow keywords, then fall back to any non-reserved key
   148	        candidates = [
   149	            k for k in step
   150	            if k not in self.RESERVED_KEYWORDS and k not in self.SERIALIZATION_OPERATORS
   151	        ]
   152	
   153	        if candidates:
   154	            # Prioritize known workflow keywords in order
   155	            matched_key: str | None = None
   156	            for workflow_key in self.WORKFLOW_KEYWORDS:
   157	                if workflow_key in candidates:
   158	                    matched_key = workflow_key
   159	                    break
   160	
   161	            # If no priority keyword found, pick the first candidate
   162	            key = matched_key if matched_key is not None else candidates[0]
   163	
   164	            operator = self._deserialize_operator(step[key])
   165	            return ParsedStep(
   166	                operator=operator,
   167	                keyword=key,
   168	                step_type=StepType.WORKFLOW,
   169	                original_step=step,
   170	                metadata={"params": step.get("params", {})},
   171	                force_layout=force_layout
   172	            )
   173	
   174	        # No recognized key - try to deserialize the whole dict
   175	        operator = deserialize_component(step)
   176	        return ParsedStep(
   177	            operator=operator,
   178	            keyword="",
   179	            step_type=StepType.SERIALIZED,
   180	            original_step=step,
   181	            metadata={},
   182	            force_layout=force_layout
   183	        )
   184	
   185	    def _parse_string_step(self, step: str) -> ParsedStep:
   186	        """Parse string step configuration."""
   187	        # For strings, we can't easily distinguish between keyword and class path
   188	        # unless we check against a list.
   189	        # But we want to avoid hardcoded lists.
   190	        # If it looks like a class path (contains dots), treat as serialized.
   191	        # If it's a single word, treat as keyword/workflow.
   192	
   193	        # Detect Python repr output from json.dumps(default=str), e.g.
   194	        # "<nirs4all.pipeline.execution.refit.executor._FullTrainFoldSplitter object at 0x...>"
   195	        # These are non-reconstructable internal objects — skip them.
   196	        if step.startswith("<") and step.endswith(">"):
   197	            return ParsedStep(
   198	                operator=None,
   199	                keyword="",
   200	                step_type=StepType.UNKNOWN,
   201	                original_step=step,
   202	                metadata={"skip": True}
   203	            )
   204	
   205	        if "." in step:
   206	             # Deserialize as a class/function reference
   207	            operator = deserialize_component(step)
   208	            return ParsedStep(
   209	                operator=operator,
   210	                keyword=step,
   211	                step_type=StepType.SERIALIZED,
   212	                original_step=step,
   213	                metadata={}
   214	            )
   215	        else:
   216	            # Treat as keyword
   217	            return ParsedStep(
   218	                operator=None,
   219	                keyword=step,
   220	                step_type=StepType.WORKFLOW,
   221	                original_step=step,
   222	                metadata={}
   223	            )
   224	
   225	    def _deserialize_operator(self, value: Any) -> Any | None:
   226	        """Deserialize an operator value if needed.
   227	
   228	        Handles:
   229	        - None: returns None
   230	        - Instances: returns as-is
   231	        - Class types: returns as-is (controller will instantiate)
   232	        - Dict with 'class'/'function': deserializes component
   233	        - String: deserializes as module path
   234	        - List/tuple: recursively deserializes each element
   235	        """
   236	        if value is None:
   237	            return None
   238	
   239	        # Handle lists/tuples (for chained operators like y_processing)
   240	        if isinstance(value, (list, tuple)):
   241	            deserialized = [self._deserialize_operator(v) for v in value]
   242	            return deserialized if isinstance(value, list) else tuple(deserialized)
   243	
   244	        # Already an instance or class type - return as-is
   245	        if not isinstance(value, (dict, str)):
   246	            return value
   247	
   248	        # Dictionary with class/function
   249	        if isinstance(value, dict):
   250	            if '_runtime_instance' in value:
   251	                return value['_runtime_instance']
   252	            if 'class' in value or 'function' in value or 'instance' in value:
   253	                deserialized = deserialize_component(value)
   254	                if deserialized is value:
   255	                    component_ref = (
   256	                        value.get('class')
   257	                        or value.get('function')
   258	                        or value.get('instance')
   259	                    )
   260	                    raise ValueError(
   261	                        f"Could not deserialize component '{component_ref}'. "
   262	                        "Check that the import path is correct."
   263	                    )
   264	                return deserialized
   265	            # Try to deserialize the whole dict
   266	            return deserialize_component(value)
   267	
   268	        # String reference
   269	        if isinstance(value, str):
   270	            return deserialize_component(value)
   271	
   272	        return value
