    25	
    26	- **Store-based** (preferred): pass `chain_id` to replay a stored chain directly from the workspace.
    27	- **Model-based**: pass `model` (bundle path, prediction dict, or config path).
    28	
    29	`model` and `chain_id` are mutually exclusive.
    30	
    31	See: {doc}`/user_guide/predictions/making_predictions`
    32	
    33	### nirs4all.run()
    34	
    35	```python
    36	nirs4all.run(
    37	    pipeline,            # List of steps, dict, path, or PipelineConfigs
    38	    dataset,             # Path, arrays, dict, SpectroDataset, or DatasetConfigs
    39	    *,
    40	    name="",
    41	    session=None,
    42	    verbose=1,
    43	    save_artifacts=True,
    44	    save_charts=True,
    45	    plots_visible=False,
    46	    random_state=None,
    47	    **runner_kwargs,
    48	) -> RunResult
    49	```
    50	
    51	See: {doc}`/user_guide/predictions/analyzing_results`
    52	
    53	### nirs4all.retrain()
    54	
    55	```python
    56	nirs4all.retrain(
    57	    source,              # Prediction dict, path to .n4a bundle, or config path
    58	    data,                # New dataset
    59	    *,
    60	    mode="full",         # "full", "transfer", or "finetune"
    61	    name="retrain_dataset",
    62	    new_model=None,
    63	    epochs=None,
    64	    session=None,
    65	    verbose=1,
    66	    save_artifacts=True,
    67	    **kwargs,
    68	) -> RunResult
    69	```
    70	
    71	See: {doc}`/user_guide/predictions/advanced_predictions`
    72	
    73	### nirs4all.explain()
    74	
    75	```python
    76	nirs4all.explain(
    77	    model,               # Prediction dict, path to .n4a bundle, or config path
    78	    data,                # Data to explain
    79	    *,
    80	    name="explain_dataset",
    81	    session=None,
    82	    verbose=1,
    83	    plots_visible=True,
    84	    n_samples=None,
    85	    explainer_type="auto",
    86	    **shap_params,
    87	) -> ExplainResult
    88	```
    89	
    90	See: {doc}`/user_guide/predictions/advanced_predictions`
    91	
    92	---
    93	
    94	## Result Classes
    95	
    96	### RunResult
    97	
    98	Returned by `nirs4all.run()` and `nirs4all.retrain()`.
    99	
   100	**Properties:**
   101	
   102	| Property | Type | Description |
   103	|----------|------|-------------|
   104	| `best` | dict | Best prediction entry (ranked by validation score) |
   105	| `best_score` | float | Best model's primary test score |
   106	| `best_rmse` | float | Best model's RMSE (NaN if unavailable) |
   107	| `best_r2` | float | Best model's R2 (NaN if unavailable) |
   108	| `best_accuracy` | float | Best model's accuracy (NaN if unavailable) |
   109	| `num_predictions` | int | Total number of predictions |
   110	| `artifacts_path` | Path or None | Path to run artifacts directory |
   111	
   112	**Methods:**
   113	
   114	| Method | Returns | Description |
   115	|--------|---------|-------------|
   116	| `top(n, **kwargs)` | PredictionResultsList | Top N predictions by ranking |
   117	| `filter(**kwargs)` | list[dict] | Filter predictions by criteria |
   118	| `get_datasets()` | list[str] | Unique dataset names |
   119	| `get_models()` | list[str] | Unique model names |
   120	| `export(output_path, format="n4a", source=None, chain_id=None)` | Path | Export model to bundle |
   121	| `export_model(output_path, source=None, format=None, fold=None)` | Path | Export model artifact only |
   122	| `summary()` | str | Multi-line summary string |
   123	| `validate(...)` | dict | Check for common issues |
   124	
   125	**top() keyword arguments:**
   126	
   127	- `rank_metric`: Metric to rank by (default: stored metric)
   128	- `rank_partition`: Partition to rank on (default: `"val"`)
   129	- `display_metrics`: List of additional metrics to compute for display
   130	- `display_partition`: Partition for display metrics (default: `"test"`)
   131	- `ascending`: Sort order (None infers from metric)
   132	- `group_by`: Group results by column(s) -- returns top N per group
   133	- `return_grouped`: If True with group_by, return dict of group to results
   134	- `aggregate`: Aggregate predictions by metadata column or `"y"`
   135	- `aggregate_method`: `"mean"`, `"median"`, or `"vote"`
   136	
   137	### PredictResult
   138	
   139	Returned by `nirs4all.predict()`.
   140	
   141	**Attributes:**
   142	
   143	| Attribute | Type | Description |
   144	|-----------|------|-------------|
   145	| `y_pred` | numpy.ndarray | Predicted values |
   146	| `metadata` | dict | Additional prediction metadata |
   147	| `sample_indices` | numpy.ndarray or None | Indices of predicted samples |
   148	| `model_name` | str | Name of the model used |
   149	| `preprocessing_steps` | list[str] | Preprocessing steps applied |
   150	
   151	**Properties:**
   152	
   153	| Property | Type | Description |
   154	|----------|------|-------------|
   155	| `values` | numpy.ndarray | Alias for y_pred |
   156	| `shape` | tuple | Shape of prediction array |
   157	| `is_multioutput` | bool | True if multi-output prediction |
   158	
   159	**Methods:**
   160	
   161	| Method | Returns | Description |
   162	|--------|---------|-------------|
   163	| `to_numpy()` | numpy.ndarray | Predictions as numpy array |
   164	| `to_list()` | list[float] | Predictions as Python list |
   165	| `to_dataframe(include_indices=True)` | pandas.DataFrame | Predictions as DataFrame |
   166	| `flatten()` | numpy.ndarray | Flattened 1D predictions |
   167	
   168	### ExplainResult
   169	
   170	Returned by `nirs4all.explain()`.
   171	
   172	**Attributes:**
   173	
   174	| Attribute | Type | Description |
   175	|-----------|------|-------------|
   176	| `shap_values` | Any | SHAP values (Explanation or ndarray) |
   177	| `feature_names` | list[str] or None | Feature names |
   178	| `base_value` | float or ndarray or None | Baseline prediction |
   179	| `visualizations` | dict[str, Path] | Generated plot files |
   180	| `explainer_type` | str | SHAP explainer type used |
   181	| `model_name` | str | Explained model name |
   182	| `n_samples` | int | Number of samples explained |
   183	
   184	**Properties:**
   185	
   186	| Property | Type | Description |
   187	|----------|------|-------------|
   188	| `values` | numpy.ndarray | Raw SHAP values array |
   189	| `shape` | tuple | Shape of SHAP values |
   190	| `mean_abs_shap` | numpy.ndarray | Mean absolute SHAP per feature |
   191	| `top_features` | list[str] | Features sorted by importance (descending) |
   192	
   193	**Methods:**
   194	
   195	| Method | Returns | Description |
   196	|--------|---------|-------------|
   197	| `get_feature_importance(top_n=None, normalize=False)` | dict[str, float] | Feature importance ranking |
   198	| `get_sample_explanation(idx)` | dict[str, float] | SHAP values for one sample |
   199	| `to_dataframe(include_feature_names=True)` | pandas.DataFrame | SHAP values as DataFrame |
   200	
   201	---
   202	
   203	## PredictionResultsList
   204	
   205	Returned by `RunResult.top()` and `Predictions.top()`. Extends Python's built-in `list` with additional methods.
   206	
   207	**Methods:**
   208	
   209	| Method | Returns | Description |
   210	|--------|---------|-------------|
   211	| `save(path="results", filename=None)` | None | Save all predictions to structured CSV |
   212	| `get(prediction_id)` | PredictionResult or None | Retrieve prediction by ID |
   213	
   214	Supports all standard list operations: indexing, slicing, iteration, `len()`, etc.
   215	
   216	## PredictionResult
   217	
   218	A dict subclass representing a single prediction. Returned as elements of `PredictionResultsList`.
   219	
   220	**Properties:**
   221	
   222	| Property | Type | Description |
   223	|----------|------|-------------|
   224	| `id` | str | Prediction identifier |
   225	| `dataset_name` | str | Dataset name |

     1	# AI Coding Assistant Onboarding
     2	
     3	**Short reference for writing nirs4all pipelines and outputting results.**
     4	
     5	This guide is intentionally narrow. It covers:
     6	- how to write pipelines,
     7	- how to expand them with generators,
     8	- how to run them,
     9	- how to inspect/export results,
    10	- how to chart them with `PredictionAnalyzer`.
    11	
    12	It does **not** cover SHAP, synthetic data generation, retraining, session internals, or architecture.
    13	
    14	**Version**: 0.8.6 | **Python**: 3.11+ | **License**: CeCILL-2.1
    15	
    16	---
    17	
    18	## 1. Fast Path
    19	
    20	Use this as the default pattern:
    21	
    22	```python
    23	import nirs4all
    24	from nirs4all.operators.transforms import StandardNormalVariate as SNV
    25	from nirs4all.operators.transforms import FirstDerivative
    26	from nirs4all.visualization.predictions import PredictionAnalyzer
    27	from sklearn.cross_decomposition import PLSRegression
    28	from sklearn.model_selection import ShuffleSplit
    29	
    30	pipeline = [
    31	    SNV(),
    32	    FirstDerivative(),
    33	    ShuffleSplit(n_splits=5, test_size=0.2, random_state=42),
    34	    PLSRegression(n_components=10),
    35	]
    36	
    37	result = nirs4all.run(
    38	    pipeline=pipeline,
    39	    dataset="sample_data/regression",
    40	    name="snv_d1_pls",
    41	    random_state=42,
    42	    verbose=1,
    43	)
    44	
    45	print(result.best["model_name"])
    46	print(result.best_rmse)
    47	print(result.best_r2)
    48	
    49	analyzer = PredictionAnalyzer(result.predictions)
    50	analyzer.plot_top_k(k=5, rank_metric="rmse")
    51	analyzer.plot_heatmap(
    52	    x_var="model_name",
    53	    y_var="preprocessings",
    54	    rank_metric="rmse",
    55	    display_metric="rmse",
    56	)
    57	
    58	result.export("exports/best_model.n4a")
    59	```
    60	
    61	Default workflow: `write pipeline -> run pipeline -> inspect RunResult -> chart with PredictionAnalyzer -> export bundle or tables`
    62

    72	    verbose=1,
    73	    random_state=None,
    74	    refit=True,
    75	    save_artifacts=True,
    76	    workspace_path="workspace",
    77	    max_generation_count=10000,
    78	)
    79	```

     1	# Configuration Reference

     3	This section documents configuration objects used to customize nirs4all behavior.
     4	
     5	## Available Configurations
     6	
     7	```{toctree}
     8	:maxdepth: 1
     9	
    10	cache_config
    11	```
    12	
    13	::::{grid} 2
    14	:gutter: 3
    15	
    16	:::{grid-item-card} CacheConfig
    17	:link: cache_config
    18	:link-type: doc
    19	
    20	Configure step-level caching and memory optimization for pipeline execution.
    21	:::
    22	
    23	::::
    24	
    25	## Usage Pattern
    26	
    27	Configuration objects are passed to API functions like `nirs4all.run()`:
    28	
    29	```python
    30	from nirs4all.config.cache_config import CacheConfig
    31	
    32	result = nirs4all.run(
    33	    pipeline=pipeline,
    34	    dataset=dataset,
    35	    cache=CacheConfig(step_cache_enabled=True),
    36	)
    37	```
    38	
    39	Most configurations are optional and use sensible defaults.

   976	---
   977	
   978	## 4. Implementation details and utilities
   979	
   980	### 4.1 Utility functions
   981	
   982	Create a small internal module for common operations:
   983	
   984	* 1D convolution with reflection padding:
   985	
   986	  ```python
   987	  def conv1d_reflect(x: np.ndarray, kernel: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
   988	      ...
   989	  ```
   990	* Gaussian kernel factory:
   991	
   992	  ```python
   993	  def gaussian_kernel(size: int, sigma: float) -> np.ndarray:
   994	      ...
   995	  ```
   996	* Safe interpolation:
   997	
   998	  ```python
   999	  def interpolate_to_axis(
  1000	      x: np.ndarray,
  1001	      lambda_src: np.ndarray,
  1002	      lambda_dst: np.ndarray,
  1003	      fill_value: float = "edge",
  1004	  ) -> np.ndarray:
  1005	      ...
  1006	  ```
  1007	
  1008	### 4.2 Parameter validation
  1009	
  1010	Each augmenter should validate ranges in `__init__`:
  1011	
  1012	* Ensure min ≤ max for ranges.
  1013	* Ensure widths and kernel sizes are positive integers.
  1014	* Raise clear `ValueError` with short messages (for config debugging).
  1015	
  1016	---
  1017	
  1018	## 5. Integration into `nirs4all` pipelines
  1019	
  1020	* Expose all classes in a dedicated module, e.g. `nirs4all.operators.augmentation`.
  1021	
  1022	* Provide **factory functions** or configuration keys to instantiate from JSON/YAML:
  1023	
  1024	  ```yaml
  1025	  - type: GaussianAdditiveNoise
  1026	    params:
  1027	      sigma: 0.02
  1028	      smoothing_kernel_width: 7
  1029	  - type: WavelengthShift
  1030	    params:
  1031	      shift_range: [-1.0, 1.0]
  1032	  ```
  1033	
  1034	* Ensure compatibility with:
  1035	
  1036	  * Existing dataset abstraction (`SpectraDataset` / `SpectroDataset`).
  1037	  * Any `TrainOnlyWrapper` or pipeline-level mechanism that passes `is_training=True` only during training.
  1038	
  1039	---
  1040	
  1041	## 6. Testing guidelines
  1042	
  1043	For each augmenter:
  1044	
  1045	1. **Shape invariance:** `X_aug.shape == X.shape`.
  1046	2. **Determinism:** fixed `random_state` ⇒ identical outputs.
  1047	3. **Amplitude sanity:** output values stay in reasonable bounds for typical NIRS ranges.
  1048	4. **No NaN / inf:** unless explicitly requested (should not be).
  1049	5. **Wavelength handling:** wavelength-aware operators receive wavelengths automatically from the controller via kwargs.
  1050	
  1051	Once implemented, add small end-to-end tests combining several augmenters in a pipeline to ensure they compose correctly.
  1052

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Configuration Reference
     2	
     3	This page provides the complete specification for pipeline and dataset configuration.
     4	
     5	## Pipeline Configuration
     6	
     7	The pipeline definition specifies the processing steps: preprocessing, cross-validation, and models.
     8	
     9	### Usage
    10	
    11	Pipeline definitions are passed directly to `nirs4all.run()` as a list, dict, or path to a YAML/JSON file. You do not need to instantiate `PipelineConfigs` manually.
    12	
    13	#### List of Steps (Recommended)
    14	
    15	```python
    16	import nirs4all
    17	from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
    18	from sklearn.cross_decomposition import PLSRegression
    19	from sklearn.model_selection import ShuffleSplit
    20	
    21	pipeline = [
    22	    MinMaxScaler(),
    23	    ShuffleSplit(n_splits=3),
    24	    {"model": PLSRegression(n_components=10)}
    25	]
    26	
    27	result = nirs4all.run(pipeline=pipeline, dataset="data/", name="MyPipeline")
    28	```
    29	
    30	#### Dictionary with Pipeline Key
    31	
    32	```python
    33	pipeline = {
    34	    "pipeline": [
    35	        MinMaxScaler(),
    36	        ShuffleSplit(n_splits=3),
    37	        {"model": PLSRegression(n_components=10)}
    38	    ]
    39	}
    40	
    41	result = nirs4all.run(pipeline=pipeline, dataset="data/", name="MyPipeline")
    42	```
    43	
    44	#### YAML File Path
    45	
    46	```python
    47	result = nirs4all.run(pipeline="config/pipeline.yaml", dataset="data/", name="MyPipeline")
    48	```
    49	
    50	**pipeline.yaml:**
    51	```yaml
    52	pipeline:
    53	  - class: sklearn.preprocessing.MinMaxScaler
    54	  - class: sklearn.model_selection.ShuffleSplit
    55	    params:
    56	      n_splits: 3
    57	  - model:
    58	      class: sklearn.cross_decomposition.PLSRegression
    59	      params:
    60	        n_components: 10
    61	```
    62	
    63	#### JSON File Path
    64	
    65	```python
    66	result = nirs4all.run(pipeline="config/pipeline.json", dataset="data/", name="MyPipeline")
    67	```
    68	
    69	### Step Serialization
    70	
    71	Steps are serialized to a canonical format:
    72	
    73	| Input | Serialized Form |
    74	|-------|-----------------|
    75	| `MinMaxScaler()` | `{"class": "sklearn.preprocessing.MinMaxScaler"}` |
    76	| `PLSRegression(n_components=10)` | `{"class": "...", "params": {"n_components": 10}}` |
    77	| `{"model": PLSRegression()}` | `{"model": {"class": "..."}}` |
    78	
    79	---
    80	
    81	## DatasetConfigs
    82	
    83	`DatasetConfigs` defines how to load and configure datasets.
    84	
    85	### Constructor
    86	
    87	```python
    88	from nirs4all.data import DatasetConfigs
    89	
    90	dataset = DatasetConfigs(
    91	    configurations,              # Path(s) or configuration dict(s)
    92	    task_type="auto",            # Force task type
    93	    signal_type=None,            # Override signal type
    94	    aggregate=None,              # Aggregation column or True
    95	    aggregate_method=None,       # Aggregation method
    96	    aggregate_exclude_outliers=None  # Exclude outliers before aggregation
    97	)
    98	```
    99	
   100	### Parameters
   101	
   102	| Parameter | Type | Default | Description |
   103	|-----------|------|---------|-------------|
   104	| `configurations` | str, dict, list | *required* | Path, config dict, or list of either |
   105	| `task_type` | str, list | `"auto"` | Task type per dataset |
   106	| `signal_type` | str, list | `None` | Signal type override |
   107	| `aggregate` | str, bool, list | `None` | Aggregation setting |
   108	| `aggregate_method` | str, list | `None` | Method: "mean", "median", "vote" |
   109	| `aggregate_exclude_outliers` | bool, list | `None` | Exclude outliers via T² |
   110	
   111	### Configuration Dictionary Keys
   112	
   113	#### Data File Keys
   114	
   115	| Key | Description | Example |
   116	|-----|-------------|---------|
   117	| `train_x` | Training features | `"spectra_train.csv"` |
   118	| `train_y` | Training targets | `"targets_train.csv"` |
   119	| `train_m` | Training metadata | `"metadata_train.csv"` |
   120	| `test_x` | Test features | `"spectra_test.csv"` |

- The canonical API pieces in §3 are real: `run(pipeline, dataset, ...)` exists ([run.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/nirs4all/api/run.py:192)); `generate.regression()` is exposed on the namespace ([generate.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/nirs4all/api/generate.py:914)); dict model steps are parsed via workflow keys like `model` ([parser.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/nirs4all/pipeline/steps/parser.py:146)); `RunResult.best_rmse` exists ([result.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/nirs4all/api/result.py:333)).
- Several migration choices are sane: `scoring_and_refit.md` is genuinely explanatory, not a recipe page ([scoring_and_refit.md](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/user_guide/scoring_and_refit.md:1)); `controllers_intro.md` is developer/contributor content ([controllers_intro.md](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/onboarding/controllers_intro.md:214)).

**Corrections / Risks**
1. **Sphinx-gallery over all examples is not currently feasible.** The proposal says the ~80 examples are rendered by sphinx-gallery and already double as integration tests ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:134)), but `sphinx-gallery` is not in docs deps ([pyproject.toml](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/pyproject.toml:142), [docs reqs](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/readthedocs.requirements.txt:1)), current examples are run only after `cd examples` ([examples.yml](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/.github/workflows/examples.yml:70)), and many scripts depend on relative `sample_data/...` paths ([U01_hello_world.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/examples/user/01_getting_started/U01_hello_world.py:71)). A gallery build must either normalize cwd/paths and skip heavy examples, or it will fail/balloon CI.

2. **“Examples already double as integration tests” is overclaimed.** `run.sh` is a hard-coded manifest, not disk-derived; it omits at least `examples/user/04_models/U06_tabpfn_nirs.py` from the user model list ([run.sh](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/examples/run.sh:83), [U06](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/examples/user/04_models/U06_tabpfn_nirs.py:1)). The proposal’s “disk-derived manifest” is a necessary prerequisite, not a current fact.

3. **The style lint spec misses the dominant violation shape.** §5 only flags assigned pipeline variables passed positionally as the first arg ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:126)). I counted 281 `pipeline=<var>` keyword passes, e.g. [logging.md](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/user_guide/logging.md:21) and [U01_hello_world.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/examples/user/01_getting_started/U01_hello_world.py:50). The lint must catch assigned list literals later passed by keyword to `run`, `Session`, or `session`, with explicit allowlist handling.

4. **The Get Started snippet is API-valid but not actually copy-paste complete.** §3 calls it the “literal first copy-paste” ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:87)), but the shown block omits `import nirs4all` and sklearn imports. Add the imports to the literalinclude file, and preferably use `random_state` plus a single-target generation form if you want deterministic beginner output.

5. **Autosummary-recursive is underspecified and mislabeled.** The proposal calls the 357 files “API symbols” ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:19)), but they are module stubs: 357 `.rst` files, 356 `automodule` directives. Current docs use `sphinx.ext.apidoc`, not autosummary ([conf.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/conf.py:10)), and optional backend modules import TensorFlow/Torch/JAX at module import time in places ([generic.py](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/nirs4all/operators/models/tensorflow/generic.py:1)). Keep `autodoc_mock_imports`/skip patterns, or autosummary will be fragile.

6. **The migration map is not page-by-page and has count contradictions.** It claims “140 dispositions” ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:170)), but the table has 89 disposition rows and many grouped catchalls. It also says 14 deletions, while explicit deletions already sum to more if `DELETE×7`, `DELETE/MERGE`, notebook deletion, and API page deletions are counted ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:279)). The “13 new pages” list includes the 13-lesson tutorial rail plus plural estates/pages ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:291)).

7. **At least one existing docs page is omitted from the §9 map.** `docs/source/ai_onboarding.md` exists and is in the current toctree ([index.md](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/index.md:146)), but it has no row in the migration map; it appears only in earlier prose. Root/meta scope from the audit also included `CHANGELOG`, `CONTRIBUTING`, and `AGENTS`, but §9 only covers README/CLAUDE/INSTALLATION ([audit](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/02_audit.md:59)).

8. **Some dispositions are too coarse to execute safely.** `augmentation/augmentations.md` is not just a how-to with a stray “Developer guidelines” header; it contains implementation details, factory/config guidance, and testing guidelines ([augmentations.md](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/source/user_guide/augmentation/augmentations.md:978)). It needs a split across Reference and Contributing, not merely a How-to rewrite.

9. **Roadmap sequencing conflicts with its own rationale.** P1 says style sweep before P3 “don’t sweep soon-to-be-deleted pages” ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:300)), but P3 is where pages are deleted/merged ([proposal](/home/delete/nirs4all/nirs4all/docs/_internal/doc_overhaul_2026-06-04/03_restructuring_proposal.md:302)). Either scope P1 to survivor pages/examples, or move the full sweep after structural migration.

10. **“Structurally impossible” is too strong.** Deleting `api/` and adding generated reference helps, but drift still re-enters through handwritten contract pages, docstrings, gallery skip lists, allowlists, and generated pages that expose internals. The proposal should replace “by construction” claims with concrete gates and ownership rules.
